  &lt;body&gt;
    &lt;p&gt;
&lt;b&gt;&lt;span style=&quot;color:#990000; font-size:18pt;&quot;&gt;Duration Simulation&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/b&gt;

    &lt;/p&gt;

    &lt;p&gt;
&amp;#160;

    &lt;/p&gt;

    &lt;p&gt;
This sample demonstrates a simulation of activities containing actions which have a duration constraint. Cameo Simulation Toolkit uses &lt;b&gt;min&lt;/b&gt; and &lt;b&gt;max&lt;/b&gt; durations of the duration constraint for simulating the time spent on the action, depending on the duration simulation mode in simulation configuration. Four duration simulation modes are supported by Cameo Simulation Toolkit which are min, max, average and random (See more information in &lt;a href=&quot;file://manual/Cameo Simulation Toolkit UserGuide.pdf&quot;&gt;Cameo Simulation Toolkit User Guide&lt;/a&gt;).

    &lt;/p&gt;

    &lt;p&gt;
&amp;#160;

    &lt;/p&gt;

    &lt;p&gt;
&lt;b&gt;&lt;span style=&quot;color:#990000;&quot;&gt;Duration Checking on Call Behavior Action&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/b&gt;

    &lt;/p&gt;

    &lt;p&gt;
&amp;#160;

    &lt;/p&gt;

    &lt;p&gt;
For a call behavior action, if it has a duration constraint applied, Cameo Simulation&amp;#160;Toolkit will use the duration constraint to validate the time spent on the called activity. If the time which is spent on the called activity is out of the range of the duration constraint, the call behavior action fails.

    &lt;/p&gt;

&lt;/body&gt;
&lt;/html&gt;</text>

  &lt;body&gt;
    &lt;p&gt;
&lt;b&gt;&lt;span style=&quot;color:#990000;&quot;&gt;Duration of activity with different scenarios&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/b&gt;

    &lt;/p&gt;

    &lt;p&gt;
&amp;#160;

    &lt;/p&gt;

    &lt;p&gt;
At the end of the each activity simulation, Cameo Simulation Toolkit will print the total duration of the activity to the simulation console. The total duration is calculated from duration on visited actions in the activity during simulation. So, the total duration depends on the scenario.

    &lt;/p&gt;

    &lt;p&gt;
&amp;#160;

    &lt;/p&gt;

    &lt;p&gt;
In this project, there are two scenarios of &lt;b&gt;go to work&lt;/b&gt; which depends on the value of &lt;b&gt;winter&lt;/b&gt;, a boolean property of &lt;b&gt;Environment&lt;/b&gt; block. Two different simulation configurations, &lt;a href=&quot;mdel://_18_1_be00301_1417411098683_351406_20103&quot;&gt;summer&lt;/a&gt; and &lt;a href=&quot;mdel://_18_1_be00301_1417411442776_714873_20211&quot;&gt;winter&lt;/a&gt;, are provided for the scenarios. You can run them to see the total duration of each scenario.

    &lt;/p&gt;

    &lt;p&gt;
